SELECT convert(DATETIME, convert(DATETIME, Rtrim(ltrim('20180327')),'yyyymmdd',10),'dd-MM-yyyy') 

SELECT ROUND(DATEDIFF(DAY, getdate(), CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), CAST(Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)) AS DATETIME), 110)),2)

SELECT Round((Convert(float, Getdate()) - CONVERT(FLOAT, CONVERT(DATETIME, Rtrim(ltrim('20180303')),'yyyymmdd')))) AS SAMPLE

Select  Rtrim(ltrim(Arcus.Idcust)) Idcust, Rtrim(ltrim (Arcus.Namecust)) Custname, 
        Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Idinvc)) Invoice_No,
        (select rtrim(ltrim(arcuso_2.value)) from CWL002.dbo.arcuso arcuso_2 where arcus.idcust=arcuso_2.idcust and Arcuso_2.Optfield='XSALESDEPT') Selling_station,
        CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), CAST(Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)) AS DATETIME), 110) Datedue,
        CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), CAST(Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Dateinvc)) AS DATETIME), 110)  Invoice_Date,    
        isnull(rtrim(ltrim(arobl.codecurn)),rtrim(ltrim(arcus.codecurn))) Currency_Code,
        arcus.Idgrp,
        Arobl.Amtduehc,
        Arobl.Amtduetc,
        Rtrim(ltrim(Arcus.Codeterm)) Codeterm,
        Arcus.Amtcrlimt,
        Arcus.Amtbalduet,
        Arcus.Amtbaldueh,
        (select Rtrim(ltrim(Arcuso.Value)) from CWL002.dbo.Arcuso Arcuso where Arcus.Idcust=Arcuso.Idcust and Arcuso.Optfield='XIDOWNER') Station_Id,
        (select rtrim(ltrim(Arcuso_1.value)) from CWL002.dbo.Arcuso Arcuso_1 where Arcus.Idcust=Arcuso_1.Idcust And Arcuso_1.Optfield='XIDPARTY') Customer_Partyid,
        ROUND(DATEDIFF(DAY, getdate(), CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), CAST(Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)) AS DATETIME), 110)),2) Days_Pastdue,
        (Case When (ROUND(DATEDIFF(DAY, getdate(), CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), CAST(Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)) AS DATETIME), 110)),2)) <0     And Arobl.Amtduetc > 0)  Then Arobl.Amtduetc Else 0 End) Current_Balance,
        (Case When (ROUND(DATEDIFF(DAY, getdate(), CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), CAST(Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)) AS DATETIME), 110)),2)) >= 0   And (ROUND(DATEDIFF(DAY, getdate(), CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), CAST(Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)) AS DATETIME), 110)),2)) <= 30 And Arobl.Amtduetc > 0)  Then Arobl.Amtduetc Else 0 End) Past_Due_1_30,
        (Case When (ROUND(DATEDIFF(DAY, getdate(), CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), CAST(Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)) AS DATETIME), 110)),2)) >= 31  And (ROUND(DATEDIFF(DAY, getdate(), CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), CAST(Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)) AS DATETIME), 110)),2)) <= 60 And Arobl.Amtduetc > 0)  Then Arobl.Amtduetc Else 0 End) Past_Due_31_60,
        (Case When (ROUND(DATEDIFF(DAY, getdate(), CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), CAST(Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)) AS DATETIME), 110)),2)) >= 61  And (ROUND(DATEDIFF(DAY, getdate(), CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), CAST(Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)) AS DATETIME), 110)),2)) <=120 And Arobl.Amtduetc > 0)  Then Arobl.Amtduetc Else 0 End) Past_Due_61_120,
        (Case When (ROUND(DATEDIFF(DAY, getdate(), CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), CAST(Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)) AS DATETIME), 110)),2)) >= 121 And Arobl.Amtduetc > 0)                                                                Then Arobl.Amtduetc Else 0 End) Past_Due_Over120,
        (Case When (ROUND(DATEDIFF(DAY, getdate(), CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), CAST(Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)) AS DATETIME), 110)),2)) >= 0   And Arobl.Amtduetc > 0)                                                                Then Arobl.Amtduetc Else 0 End) Past_Due_Balance,
        (case when ( Arobl.Amtduetc < 0) Then Arobl.Amtduetc Else 0 End) Unapplied_Credits,
        (Case When (Round((Convert(float, Getdate()) - CONVERT(FLOAT, CONVERT(DATETIME, Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)),'yyyymmdd')))) < -7     And Arobl.Amtduetc > 0)  Then Arobl.Amtduetc Else 0 End) Current_Balance_LT_7,        
        (Case When (Round((Convert(float, Getdate()) - CONVERT(FLOAT, CONVERT(DATETIME, Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)),'yyyymmdd')))) >= -7   And (Round((Convert(float, Getdate()) - CONVERT(FLOAT, CONVERT(DATETIME, Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)),'yyyymmdd'))))) < 0 And Arobl.Amtduetc > 0)  Then Arobl.Amtduetc Else 0 End) Current_Balance_7_to_0,
        (Case When (Round((Convert(float, Getdate()) - CONVERT(FLOAT, CONVERT(DATETIME, Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)),'yyyymmdd')))) >=  0   And (Round((Convert(float, Getdate()) - CONVERT(FLOAT, CONVERT(DATETIME, Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)),'yyyymmdd'))))) <= 7 And Arobl.Amtduetc > 0)  Then Arobl.Amtduetc Else 0 End) Past_Due_1_7,
        (Case When (Round((Convert(float, Getdate()) - CONVERT(FLOAT, CONVERT(DATETIME, Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)),'yyyymmdd')))) >=  8   And (Round((Convert(float, Getdate()) - CONVERT(FLOAT, CONVERT(DATETIME, Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)),'yyyymmdd'))))) <= 30 And Arobl.Amtduetc > 0)  Then Arobl.Amtduetc Else 0 End) Past_Due_8_30,
        (Case When (Round((Convert(float, Getdate()) - CONVERT(FLOAT, CONVERT(DATETIME, Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)),'yyyymmdd')))) >= 61   And (Round((Convert(float, Getdate()) - CONVERT(FLOAT, CONVERT(DATETIME, Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)),'yyyymmdd'))))) <= 90 And Arobl.Amtduetc > 0)  Then Arobl.Amtduetc Else 0 End) Past_Due_61_90,
        (Case When (Round((Convert(float, Getdate()) - CONVERT(FLOAT, CONVERT(DATETIME, Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)),'yyyymmdd')))) >= 91   And (Round((Convert(float, Getdate()) - CONVERT(FLOAT, CONVERT(DATETIME, Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Datedue)),'yyyymmdd'))))) <= 120 And Arobl.Amtduetc > 0)  Then Arobl.Amtduetc Else 0 End) Past_Due_91_120,
       'CWL002' DBALIAS  , case  arobl.DATEPAID  when 0 then null else to_char(convert(DATETIME, Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.DATEPAID)),'yyyymmdd'),'dd-Mon-yyyy') end DATEPAID , 
        case  arobl.DATEPAID when 0 then 0  else (Round((Convert(float, Getdate()) - CONVERT(FLOAT, CONVERT(DATETIME, Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.Dateinvc)),'yyyymmdd')))) - Round((Convert(float, Getdate()) - CONVERT(FLOAT, CONVERT(DATETIME, Rtrim(ltrim(Arobl.DATEPAID)),'yyyymmdd'))))) end  days_to_pay,
        arobl.idcustpo,arobl.AMTINVCHC 
 From   CWL002..dbo.Arcus Arcus
    Left Outer Join CWL002..dbo Arobl Arobl     On Arcus.Idcust=Arobl.Idcust

Select R.IDCUST, R.NAMECUST, R.IDINVC, R.INVOICE_DATE, R.AMTPAYM,R.DATERMIT, R.IDRMIT,
R.REMIT_DATE, R.CODECURN,to_date(R.DATERMIT,'yyyymmdd'),
(NVL(NVL(GET_SAGE_CUR_CONV_RATE(R.CODECURN,R.REMIT_DATE),1),1)*R.AMTPAYM)  REMITAMT_USD,
R.CNTBTCH,R.CNTITEM,R.CUSTOMER_PARTYID,R.VALUE,R.COMPANYID,b.branch, b.country, b.region, b.start_date, s.selling_station, 
s.rollup_station
from CWL_SAGE_AR_CASH_RECEIPTS_V@SQLDB R, cwl_branch_rollup b, cwl_station_rollup s
where S.Rollup_Station = B.Branch
And R.datermit >= rpad(to_char(Sysdate-4,'yyyymmdd'),9)
and s.selling_station='MAGSLS' AND ROWNUM=10
ORDER BY NAMECUST, IDINVC;

SELECT DISTINCT S.SHPNO AWBNO,H.DOCAMTFC INVOICE_AMOUNT, H.CURRCODE CURRENCY,H.DOCNO INVOICE_NO,H.DOCDATE INVOICE_DATE,
S.CUSTNAME CLIENT,
FROM CWL_SHIPMENT_STATUS_V S  
LEFT OUTER JOIN KEWILLFWD.IVJOB I ON S.SHPNO=I.AWBBL
LEFT OUTER JOIN KEWILLFWD.IVHDR H ON I.DOCNO=H.DOCNO AND S.PARTYID_CUST= H.PARTYID_CUST
WHERE S.JOB_UNID= CWL_GET_UNID(S.GSHPID,'MIN') AND S.SHPNO='SINCJ0004876';

SNR Drilldown query for BI team


select * from (SELECT A.job_date,A.salesrepcode,A.docno,A.doc_date,A.house_ownerid,A.shpno,A.biztype,
A.jobno,A.chrgcode,A.charge_code,A.payeename, ROUND(A.amount, 2) amount,A.charge_type,a.lock_period,a.acct_type,
a.LOCAL_CURRCODE,a.LOCAL_AMOUNT FROM CWL_MD_SALES_DRILLDOWN_DTL4_V A 
 WHERE A.gshpid = 'G0000000000003385478'  
 order by case A.charge_type when 'Revenue' then 1 
 when 'Estimated Revenue -Unbilled' then 2 
 when 'Master Actual Allocated to House' then 3 
 when 'Actual Cost' then 4 when 'Estimated Cost - Locked' then 5 
 when 'Master Estimates Allocated to House' then 6 
 when 'Estimated Cost - Not Locked' then 7 end) x  order by charge_type desc,doc_date,docno,chrgcode asc
 
 
 
select get_all_salesstation(A.gshpid) as SELLING_STATION,A.OWNERID,A.SHPNO,A.JOBNO,A.CONSOLNO,A.CUSTNAME,A.SHPRNAME,
A.CSGNNAME, CASE WHEN A.BIZTYPE IN ('AE','AI') THEN A.POLNAME  WHEN A.BIZTYPE IN ('SE','SI','IL') THEN A.PORNAME END POLNAME, 
CASE WHEN A.BIZTYPE IN ('AE','AI') THEN A.POLCTRY  WHEN A.BIZTYPE IN ('SE','SI','IL') THEN A.PORCTRY END POLCTRY, 
CASE WHEN A.BIZTYPE IN ('AE','AI') THEN A.PODNAME  WHEN A.BIZTYPE IN ('SE','SI','IL') THEN A.devryname END PODNAME, 
CASE WHEN A.BIZTYPE IN ('AE','AI') THEN A.PODCTRY  WHEN A.BIZTYPE IN ('SE','SI','IL') THEN A.devryctry END PODCTRY,
A.SERVICELEVEL,A.SALESREPCODE,get_current_status2(A.gshpid) currentStatus,A.PROMISEDELVYDATE,
get_all_minJobdate(A.Gshpid) JOBDATE,A.BIZTYPE,A.SERVICETYPE,A.TOTCWGT,A.TOTCWGT_UT, A.gshpid  
from  cwl_shipment_status_v A   where A.UNID IN CWL_GET_UNID(A.GSHPID,'MIN') AND A.gshpid='G0000000000003385478'

select customer_partyid partyid_cust, salescode salesrep, selling_station, region, country, days_to_pay
from (
       select a.customer_partyid,  avg (a.days_to_pay) days_to_pay
       from CWL_SAGE_AR_TRIAL_BALANCE_V a 
       where  a.Invoice_Date_Df >= sysdate - 30
           and a.amtduehc = 0
           and a.amtinvchc > 0
        and  a.customer_partyid = 'JOHN425MAG' 
       group by a.customer_partyid
       ) d join cwl_selling_station_v s on s.partyid = d.customer_partyid
	   

  CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW "WEBPORTAL"."CWL_AR_DAYS_TO_PAY_MV" ("PARTYID_CUST", "SALESREP", "SELLING_STATION", "REGION", "COUNTRY", "DAYS_TO_PAY")
  ORGANIZATION HEAP PCTFREE 10 PCTUSED 40 INITRANS 1 MAXTRANS 255 
 NOCOMPRESS LOGGING
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "USERS" 
  BUILD IMMEDIATE
  USING INDEX 
  REFRESH COMPLETE ON DEMAND START WITH sysdate+0 NEXT SYSDATE + 1
  USING DEFAULT LOCAL ROLLBACK SEGMENT
  USING ENFORCED CONSTRAINTS DISABLE QUERY REWRITE
  AS select customer_partyid partyid_cust, salescode salesrep, selling_station, region, country, days_to_pay
from (
       select customer_partyid,  avg (days_to_pay) days_to_pay
       from cwl_accpac_ar_detail_v a 
       where  to_date(trim(invoice_date),'dd-Mon-yyyy') >= sysdate - 120
           and amtduehc = 0
           and amtinvchc > 0
--           and  customer_partyid = 'TEMP100BOS' 
       group by customer_partyid
       ) d join cwl_selling_station_v s on s.partyid = d.customer_partyid;

  CREATE INDEX "WEBPORTAL"."CWL_AR_DTP_IDX2" ON "WEBPORTAL"."CWL_AR_DAYS_TO_PAY_MV" ("SALESREP", "PARTYID_CUST") 
  PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "USERS" ;
  CREATE INDEX "WEBPORTAL"."CWL_AR_DTP_IDX1" ON "WEBPORTAL"."CWL_AR_DAYS_TO_PAY_MV" ("PARTYID_CUST") 
  PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "USERS" ;
  CREATE INDEX "WEBPORTAL"."CWL_AR_DTP_IDX3" ON "WEBPORTAL"."CWL_AR_DAYS_TO_PAY_MV" ("SELLING_STATION", "PARTYID_CUST") 
  PCTFREE 10 INITRANS 2 MAXTRANS 255 COMPUTE STATISTICS 
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "USERS" ;

  CWL_SAGE_AR_DAYS_TO_PAY_MV

select COUNT(distinct B.GSHPID) from cwl_otp_detail_mv B where ( (B.PROMISEDELVYDATE - nvl(B.ACT_DATE,SYSDATE)>=0  AND B.PROMISEDELVYDATE <= SYSDATE) or (SERVICELEVEL ='Next Flight Out'))  AND   B.OWNERID='HKG'  and  B.SELLING_STATION ='MAGSLS'  and  lower(B.POLCTRY)='us'  and  lower(B.PODCTRY)='hk'  and  B.JOBDATE>='01-Jul-2018'  and  B.JOBDATE<='26-Feb-2019';
select COUNT(distinct B.GSHPID) from cwl_otp_detail_mv B where  B.PROMISEDELVYDATE <= SYSDATE   and   B.OWNERID='HKG'  and  B.SELLING_STATION ='MAGSLS'  and  lower(B.POLCTRY)='us'  and  lower(B.PODCTRY)='hk'  and  B.JOBDATE>='01-Jul-2018'  and  B.JOBDATE<='26-Feb-2019';

select B.REASON_CODE,COUNT(DISTINCT B.GSHPID) from cwl_otp_detail_mv B  
where (B.PROMISEDELVYDATE < nvl(B.ACT_DATE,SYSDATE)) AND B.PROMISEDELVYDATE <= SYSDATE    
and B.REASON_CODE IS NOT NULL AND B.SERVICELEVEL  NOT IN ('Next Flight Out')  
AND (nvl(B.ACT_DATE,SYSDATE) - B.PROMISEDELVYDATE >= 1)  AND    B.OWNERID='HKG'  
and  B.SELLING_STATION ='MAGSLS'  and  lower(B.POLCTRY)='us'  and  lower(B.PODCTRY)='hk'  
and  B.JOBDATE>='01-Jul-2018'  and  B.JOBDATE<='26-Feb-2019'  group by B.REASON_CODE;

select B.REASON_CODE,COUNT(DISTINCT B.GSHPID) COUNT from cwl_otp_detail_mv B 
where B.PROMISEDELVYDATE <= SYSDATE  AND  (B.reason_code  like 'OTP%' or B.reason_code is null)  
AND (nvl(B.ACT_DATE,SYSDATE) - B.PROMISEDELVYDATE >= 1)
AND B.SERVICELEVEL  NOT IN ('Next Flight Out') AND    B.OWNERID='HKG'  
and  B.SELLING_STATION ='MAGSLS'  and  lower(B.POLCTRY)='us'  and  lower(B.PODCTRY)='hk' 
and  B.JOBDATE>='01-Jul-2018'  and  B.JOBDATE<='26-Feb-2019'  group by B.REASON_CODE;

select 1 as days, B.REASON_CODE,COUNT(DISTINCT B.GSHPID) COUNT from cwl_otp_detail_mv B where  
(B.PROMISEDELVYDATE - nvl(B.ACT_DATE,SYSDATE)>=2)  AND B.PROMISEDELVYDATE <= SYSDATE  
AND B.SERVICELEVEL  NOT IN ('Next Flight Out')   AND   B.OWNERID='HKG' 
and  B.SELLING_STATION ='MAGSLS'  and  lower(B.POLCTRY)='us' 
and  lower(B.PODCTRY)='hk'  and  B.JOBDATE>='01-Jul-2018'  and  B.JOBDATE<='26-Feb-2019'
group by B.REASON_CODE 
Union All select 2 as days, B.REASON_CODE,COUNT(DISTINCT B.GSHPID) COUNT from cwl_otp_detail_mv B where 
(B.PROMISEDELVYDATE - nvl(B.ACT_DATE,SYSDATE) =1)  AND B.PROMISEDELVYDATE <= SYSDATE  AND B.SERVICELEVEL  
NOT IN ('Next Flight Out')   AND   B.OWNERID='HKG'  and  B.SELLING_STATION ='MAGSLS'  
and  lower(B.POLCTRY)='us'  and  lower(B.PODCTRY)='hk'  and  B.JOBDATE>='01-Jul-2018' 
and  B.JOBDATE<='26-Feb-2019'  group by B.REASON_CODE Union All select 3 as days,
B.REASON_CODE,COUNT(DISTINCT B.GSHPID) COUNT from cwl_otp_detail_mv B where   (B.PROMISEDELVYDATE - nvl(B.ACT_DATE,SYSDATE) =0)  AND B.PROMISEDELVYDATE <= SYSDATE  AND B.SERVICELEVEL  NOT IN ('Next Flight Out')   AND   B.OWNERID='HKG'  and  B.SELLING_STATION ='MAGSLS'  and  lower(B.POLCTRY)='us'  and  lower(B.PODCTRY)='hk'  and  B.JOBDATE>='01-Jul-2018'  and  B.JOBDATE<='26-Feb-2019'  group by B.REASON_CODE Union All select 4 as days, B.REASON_CODE,COUNT(DISTINCT B.GSHPID) COUNT from cwl_otp_detail_mv B where         (nvl(B.ACT_DATE,SYSDATE) - B.PROMISEDELVYDATE = 1)  AND B.PROMISEDELVYDATE <= SYSDATE  AND B.SERVICELEVEL  NOT IN ('Next Flight Out')    AND   B.OWNERID='HKG'  and  B.SELLING_STATION ='MAGSLS'  and  lower(B.POLCTRY)='us'  and  lower(B.PODCTRY)='hk'  and  B.JOBDATE>='01-Jul-2018'  and  B.JOBDATE<='26-Feb-2019'  group by B.REASON_CODE Union All select 5 as days, B.REASON_CODE,COUNT(DISTINCT B.GSHPID) COUNT from cwl_otp_detail_mv B where  (nvl(B.ACT_DATE,SYSDATE) - B.PROMISEDELVYDATE = 2)  AND B.PROMISEDELVYDATE <= SYSDATE  AND B.SERVICELEVEL  NOT IN ('Next Flight Out')    AND   B.OWNERID='HKG'  and  B.SELLING_STATION ='MAGSLS'  and  lower(B.POLCTRY)='us'  and  lower(B.PODCTRY)='hk'  and  B.JOBDATE>='01-Jul-2018'  and  B.JOBDATE<='26-Feb-2019'  group by B.REASON_CODE Union All select 6 as days, B.REASON_CODE,COUNT(DISTINCT B.GSHPID) COUNT from cwl_otp_detail_mv B where  (nvl(B.ACT_DATE,SYSDATE) - B.PROMISEDELVYDATE >= 3)  AND B.PROMISEDELVYDATE <= SYSDATE  AND B.SERVICELEVEL  NOT IN ('Next Flight Out')    AND   B.OWNERID='HKG'  and  B.SELLING_STATION ='MAGSLS'  and  lower(B.POLCTRY)='us'  and  lower(B.PODCTRY)='hk'  and  B.JOBDATE>='01-Jul-2018'  and  B.JOBDATE<='26-Feb-2019'  group by B.REASON_CODE

create or replace FUNCTION "GET_DESTINATION" (v_gshpid varchar2 )
Return varchar2
Is 
v_dest varchar2 (4000);
v_biztype varchar2 (20);
v_count number (20);
v_totcount number (20);
v_reccount number (20);
v_shiptype varchar2 (10);
-- For new changes
v_minjobunid number (20);
v_maxjobunid number (20);
v_maxunid number (20);
v_createdate date;
v_minjobdate date;
v_implementdate date;
v_origin_ctry varchar2 (20);
v_ownctry_brach varchar2 (20);
v_miamag_brach varchar2 (20);
v_dest_ctry varchar2 (20);
v_impl_ctry varchar2 (20);
v_dest_city varchar2 (20);
v_singlecount number (20);
v_ownctrycount number (20);
v_singlentry boolean:=false;
v_multibiztype boolean:=false;


Begin
  
  v_minjobunid := CWL_GET_UNID(V_Gshpid,'MIN');
    v_minjobdate := GET_MIN_JOBDATE(V_Gshpid);
  select max(unid) into v_maxjobunid  from kewillfwd.job where gshpid = V_Gshpid  and biztype != 'NJ' and voiddate is null;
   
  select jobdate into v_createdate from kewillfwd.job  where gshpid = v_gshpid 
  and unid = v_minjobunid;

  select count (distinct (substr (biztype, 1, 1))) into v_count from kewillfwd.job where gshpid = v_gshpid and biztype != 'NJ' ;  
   
      
    
    if v_count > 1 then        
      -- As per Michele comment we need to consider shptype as Ocean for Air and Ocean Shipments  
         select sum(count (distinct (substr (biztype, 1, 1)))) into v_count
           from kewillfwd.job where gshpid = v_gshpid and biztype != 'NJ' 
              group by substr (biztype, 1, 1);
        if (v_count = 2) then
          v_shiptype :='S';
          select  max(unid)  into v_maxjobunid from kewillfwd.job where gshpid=v_gshpid and  biztype in ('SE','SI') and Devryctry is not null;
          v_multibiztype := true;
        else
        select substr (biztype,1,1) into v_shiptype 
        from kewillfwd.job 
        where gshpid = v_gshpid 
          and biztype != 'NJ'
          and unid = v_minjobunid;
         end if; 
    else 
        select distinct substr (biztype,1,1) into v_shiptype 
        from kewillfwd.job 
        where gshpid = v_gshpid 
        and biztype != 'NJ';
    end if;
	 
	 		
      
        
	IF (v_shiptype ='A')  THEN
        select nvl(podctry,'xxx') into v_dest_ctry from kewillfwd.job where unid = v_minjobunid;
        select count(START_DATE) into v_reccount from CWL_MD_COUNTRY_2017 where CTRY_CODE = v_dest_ctry;
        select nvl(podcity,'xxx') into v_dest_city from kewillfwd.job where unid = v_minjobunid;
                    
  ELSIF (v_shiptype ='S' and v_multibiztype)  THEN
   
        select nvl( Devryctry,'xxx') into v_dest_ctry from kewillfwd.job where gshpid=v_gshpid and  biztype in ('SE','SI') and Devryctry is not null and rownum=1;
        select nvl( devrycity,'xxx') into v_dest_city from kewillfwd.job where gshpid=v_gshpid and biztype in ('SE','SI') and devrycity is not null and rownum=1;
        select count(START_DATE) into v_reccount from CWL_MD_COUNTRY_2017 where CTRY_CODE = v_dest_ctry;
        
  ELSE
     
        select nvl(Devryctry,'xxx') into v_dest_ctry from kewillfwd.job where unid = v_minjobunid;
        select nvl(devrycity,'xxx') into v_dest_city from kewillfwd.job where unid = v_minjobunid;
        select count(START_DATE) into v_reccount from CWL_MD_COUNTRY_2017 where CTRY_CODE = v_dest_ctry;
  END IF;
	 
	 
	 

select count(*) into v_totcount from kewillfwd.job  where gshpid = v_gshpid  and biztype != 'NJ' ; 
  

-- Multiple Entry 

	IF v_totcount > 1 then
		  
		 IF v_reccount > 0 then
				select START_DATE into v_implementdate from CWL_MD_COUNTRY_2017 where CTRY_CODE = v_dest_ctry;    
							IF v_createdate >= v_implementdate THEN   
									SELECT COUNT(distinct OWNERID) INTO v_ownctrycount FROM CWL_SHIPMENT_STATUS_V 
										WHERE Unid = v_maxjobunid and  
											OWNERID IN (SELECT distinct BRANCH FROM CWL_BRANCH_ROLLUP_2017 WHERE COUNTRY=v_dest_ctry) ;  
                       	Select distinct Ownerid Into v_ownctry_brach From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid;                  
                       IF (v_ownctrycount = 0 and v_ownctry_brach='MIAMAG' and v_dest_ctry ='US')  THEN  
                          		Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid;                      
                       ELSIF 	(v_ownctrycount = 0 and v_dest_city = 'LBU' AND v_dest_ctry='MY')  THEN
														Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid; 
															IF v_dest ='SIN' or v_dest ='KUL' then
																Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid; 
															else
																v_dest := 'CWW'; 
															end if; 
                       ELSIF 	(v_ownctrycount = 0)  THEN   
                      --   DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('else entry' || v_ownctrycount);
                                if(v_multibiztype) then
                                    select max(unid) into v_maxjobunid  from kewillfwd.job where gshpid = V_Gshpid
                                    and biztype != 'NJ' and voiddate is null;
                                    select  max(unid)  into v_maxunid from kewillfwd.job where gshpid=v_gshpid 
                                    and  biztype in ('SE','SI') and Devryctry is not null;                                    
                                    if(v_maxjobunid != v_maxunid) then                                    
                                    	SELECT COUNT(distinct OWNERID) INTO v_ownctrycount FROM CWL_SHIPMENT_STATUS_V 
                                          			WHERE Unid = v_maxjobunid and  
                                   		OWNERID IN (SELECT distinct BRANCH FROM CWL_BRANCH_ROLLUP_2017 WHERE COUNTRY=v_dest_ctry) ;  
                                           if(v_ownctrycount = 0) then
                                                 v_dest:= 'CWW';
                                           else
                                            Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid; 
                                           end if;                                   
                                    else 
                                      	v_dest := 'CWW';          
                                    end if;
                               else 
                                    	SELECT COUNT(distinct OWNERID) INTO v_ownctrycount FROM CWL_SHIPMENT_STATUS_V 
                                      WHERE Unid = v_maxjobunid and  OWNERID IN (SELECT distinct BRANCH FROM CWL_BRANCH_ROLLUP_2017 WHERE COUNTRY=v_dest_ctry) ;                               
                                      if(v_ownctrycount = 0) THEN
                                          	v_dest := 'CWW';    
                                    
                                      ELSE
                                         Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid;   
                                      END IF;
                                 
                               end if;     
											 ELSE
													Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid;      
											 END IF; 	
             ELSE
                	Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid;                     
						END IF;
            
          
            
		 ELSE
  --   DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('else entry' || v_reccount);
        select sum(count (distinct (substr (biztype, 1, 1)))) into v_count
           from kewillfwd.job where gshpid = v_gshpid and biztype != 'NJ' 
              group by substr (biztype, 1, 1);
        if  v_count = 2 then      
        	Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid  in(select max(unid)
            from kewillfwd.job where gshpid = V_Gshpid  and biztype != 'NJ' and biztype in ('SE','SI')  and voiddate is null);
      else 
       Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid;
      end if;
		 END IF;

	 
ELSIF v_totcount = 1 then
	
			IF v_reccount > 0 then
							select START_DATE into v_implementdate from CWL_MD_COUNTRY_2017 where CTRY_CODE = v_dest_ctry;  
                --   DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('v_createdate entry' || v_createdate);
                --     DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('v_implementdate entry' || v_implementdate);
									IF v_createdate >= v_implementdate THEN   
										SELECT COUNT(distinct OWNERID) INTO v_ownctrycount FROM CWL_SHIPMENT_STATUS_V 
												WHERE Unid = v_maxjobunid and  
												OWNERID IN (SELECT distinct BRANCH FROM CWL_BRANCH_ROLLUP_2017 WHERE COUNTRY=v_dest_ctry) ; 
                      	Select distinct Ownerid Into v_ownctry_brach From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid;    
                       
                       IF (v_ownctrycount = 0 and v_dest_city != 'LBU' AND v_dest_ctry !='MY' and v_ownctry_brach !='MIAMAG')  THEN  
                          	v_dest := 'CWW'; 
                       ELSIF (v_ownctrycount = 0 and v_ownctry_brach='MIAMAG' and v_dest_ctry ='US')  THEN  
                          		Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid; 
                       ELSIF 	(v_ownctrycount = 0 and v_dest_city = 'LBU' AND v_dest_ctry='MY')  THEN
                  --     DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('multiple entry' || v_ownctrycount);
														Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid; 
															IF v_dest ='SIN' or v_dest ='KUL' then
																Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid; 
															else
																v_dest := 'CWW'; 
															end if;    
                        ELSIF 	(v_ownctrycount = 0)  THEN                          
                                if(v_multibiztype) then
                                    select max(unid) into v_maxjobunid  from kewillfwd.job where gshpid = V_Gshpid
                                    and biztype != 'NJ' and voiddate is null;
                                    select  max(unid)  into v_maxunid from kewillfwd.job where gshpid=v_gshpid 
                                    and  biztype in ('SE','SI') and Devryctry is not null;
                                  --   DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('v_maxjobunid' || v_maxjobunid);
                                    --    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('v_maxunid' || v_maxunid);
                                    if(v_maxjobunid != v_maxunid) then                                     
                                      	Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid;  
                                       --   DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('inside the condition' || v_dest);
                                    else 
                                      	v_dest := 'CWW';          
                                    end if;
                               else                   
                                  	v_dest := 'CWW';   
                               end if;            
											 ELSE
													Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid;      
											 END IF; 	
                  ELSE
													Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid;                
									END IF;
		  ELSE
								 select sum(count (distinct (substr (biztype, 1, 1)))) into v_count
           from kewillfwd.job where gshpid = v_gshpid and biztype != 'NJ' 
              group by substr (biztype, 1, 1);
            --   DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('v_count entry' || v_count);
        if  v_count = 2 then      
        	Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid  in(select max(unid)
            from kewillfwd.job where gshpid = V_Gshpid  and biztype != 'NJ' and biztype in ('SE','SI')  and voiddate is null);
          --   DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('v_dest entry' || v_dest);
      else 
       Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid;
       -- DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('v_dest entry' || v_dest);
      end if;                                                         
			END IF;
	ELSE
					 select sum(count (distinct (substr (biztype, 1, 1)))) into v_count
           from kewillfwd.job where gshpid = v_gshpid and biztype != 'NJ' 
              group by substr (biztype, 1, 1);
        if  v_count = 2 then      
        	Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid  in(select max(unid)
            from kewillfwd.job where gshpid = V_Gshpid  and biztype != 'NJ' and biztype in ('SE','SI')  and voiddate is null);
      else 
       Select distinct Ownerid Into v_dest From Kewillfwd.Job Where Unid = v_maxjobunid;
      end if;    
	END IF;
 
 
 IF  v_dest ='CWW' and v_minjobdate >= '01-Jan-2017'  THEN    
      SELECT distinct ROLLUP_BRANCH INTO v_dest FROM CWL_MD_COUNTRY_2017 WHERE CTRY_CODE=v_dest_ctry;
       IF (v_dest_ctry ='CA' AND v_dest ='CWW' AND  v_minjobdate < '01-Jan-2018') then
           v_dest:='YVR';
        END IF; 
 END IF;
 
 Return v_dest;


end;

We have reviewed this issue, collection module will pull data from SAGE and TMF based on the clientID and invoice number. 

For example invoice number UCCA000921 is in SAGE database and its not there in TMF. But the partyid is updated as CANR525YYC in SAGE.

When we search with Client group that time this will pull the above invoice based on partyid even salesrep is null (since this invoice is not there in TMF). 

When we search with Salesrep code, this invoice will be filtered since  the invoice is not there in TMF.

Thats the reason  we are getting the difference.  We are working on this issue and will update the Salesrep code based on the client id for Sage Db and fix it.

update CWL_AE_ACTIONS set permanent_loss='Y', permanent_loss_status='Approved',
loss_approver_id='bmartin',loss_requestor_id='bmartin' where ae_unid in (
select distinct ae_unid from CWL_AE_ACTIONS where shpno
in (select distinct field from temp_sk_field) and action_type='Shipment with Loss');

update cwl_ae_comments set permanent_loss_flag='Y' where ae_unid
IN (
select distinct ae_unid from cwl_ae_comments where ae_unid in
(select distinct ae_unid from CWL_AE_ACTIONS where shpno in
(select distinct field from temp_sk_field) and action_type='Shipment with Loss')
and loss_comments_type is not null) and loss_comments_type is not null;

                                    //   alert(JSON.parse(responseResults).Code);
                                    let jsonObj = JSON.parse(responseResults);
                                    var rsCode = (jsonObj.Code);
                                    if (rsCode == "600") {
                                        jAlert(jsonObj.statusMsg);
                                        window.parent.validate();
                                        $("#multipleCommentsDiv").dialog("close")

                                    } else {
                                        jAlert(responseResults.statusMsg);
                                    }
                                }

  ORGANIZATION HEAP PCTFREE 10 PCTUSED 40 INITRANS 1 MAXTRANS 255 
 NOCOMPRESS LOGGING
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1
  BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "USERS" 
  BUILD IMMEDIATE
  USING INDEX

FROM CWL_PAOPS_2020_V;

create or replace function GET_TAX_AMOUNT (v_gshpid varchar2, v_partyidcust varchar2)
Return Number
Is
v_amt number;

      SELECT SUM(D.AMTBC * nvl(get_curr_conv_rate(d.currcode,d.docdate),1)) into v_amt
      FROM CWL_INVOICE_VIEW_V D 
	  WHERE d.partyid_cust = v_partyidcust 
	  AND d.job_unid in (select s.UNID from KEWILLFWD.JOB s where s.gshpid = v_gshpid)
	  AND d.partyid_cust not in ( Select Related_Party_Id From Cwl_Statistical_Party_V Where Statistical_Party_Id = 'INTERCO' )
      AND D.chrgcode in ('DGSTT', 'DIVAT', 'DNCAN', 'IOFFA', 'DVATT', 'IDUTA', 'IDUTY',
                      'IGSTT', 'IIVAT','IVATT', 'ICOGA','IMPFC','IHMFC','INVIVA');
Return V_Amt; 
end;

  SELECT DISTINCT S.GSHPID,S.SHPNO,S.OWNERID,S.JOBDATE,S.PARTYID_CUST,
DECODE(S.BIZTYPE,'AE','AIR','AI','AIR','SI','OCEAN','SE','OCEAN','IL','DOMESTIC') BIZTYPE,
S.TOTCWGT,S.TOTCWGT_UT, GET_WT_CALC(S.TOTCWGT,S.TOTCWGT_UT) TOTCWKGS,
S.TOTGWGT,S.TOTGWGT_UT, GET_WT_CALC(S.TOTGWGT,S.TOTGWGT_UT) TOTGWKGS,
CASE WHEN (GET_WT_CALC(S.TOTCWGT,S.TOTCWGT_UT) > GET_WT_CALC(S.TOTGWGT,S.TOTGWGT_UT))
THEN GET_WT_CALC(S.TOTCWGT,S.TOTCWGT_UT)
ELSE GET_WT_CALC(S.TOTGWGT,S.TOTGWGT_UT) 
END FINALKGS,
GET_BILLED_AMT_USD_CUST(S.GSHPID,S.PARTYID_CUST) INVOICE_AMOUNT,
GET_MIN_INVOICE_DATE(S.GSHPID,S.PARTYID_CUST) INVOICE_DATE,  
GET_PAID_DATE(S.GSHPID,S.PARTYID_CUST) PAID_DATE,
(GET_PAID_DATE(S.GSHPID,S.PARTYID_CUST) - GET_MIN_INVOICE_DATE(S.GSHPID,S.PARTYID_CUST)) DAYS_TO_PAY,
TO_CHAR(S.JOBDATE,'MM') JOB_MONTH, TO_CHAR(S.JOBDATE,'YYYY') JOB_YEAR, GET_FISCAL_PERIOD (S.JOBDATE) FINPERIOD,
(GET_MIN_INVOICE_DATE(S.GSHPID,S.PARTYID_CUST) - 
    NVL(Get_Delivered_Date (S.Gshpid),GET_MAX_NONDEL_DATE(S.GSHPID,get_current_milestone_code_V2(S.GSHPID)))) FINDELTOINVOICE,
GET_QUATER(TO_CHAR(S.JOBDATE,'MM')) QUATER,s.promisedelvydate,
NVL(Get_Delivered_Date (S.Gshpid),GET_MAX_NONDEL_DATE(S.GSHPID,get_current_milestone_code_V2(S.GSHPID))) ACT_DATE,
CASE WHEN (s.promisedelvydate < NVL(Get_Delivered_Date (S.Gshpid),GET_MAX_NONDEL_DATE(S.GSHPID,get_current_milestone_code_V2(S.GSHPID)))) THEN 'Late'
ELSE 'Ontime' END ONTIME,
get_pod_reason_code_v2(S.GSHPID)  REASON_CODE,
get_pod_reason_desc(S.GSHPID)  REASON_DESC,
GET_LOAD_TERM(S.JOB_UNID) LOADTERM,
GET_CONTAINER_BYTYPE(S.JOB_UNID,'20') AS TWFT,
GET_CONTAINER_BYTYPE(S.JOB_UNID,'20HC') AS TWHCFT,
GET_CONTAINER_BYTYPE(S.JOB_UNID,'40') AS FRFT,
GET_CONTAINER_BYTYPE(S.JOB_UNID,'40HC') AS FRHCFT,
GET_CONTAINER_BYTYPE(S.JOB_UNID,'45') AS FFFT
FROM CWL_SHIPMENT_STATUS_V S WHERE S.JOB_UNID = CWL_GET_UNID(S.GSHPID,'MIN')
AND (S.SERVICELEVEL != 'INVOICE' OR S.SERVICEPLANTMPL != 'INVONLY')
AND S.shpno IN ('HYYC20007021','HYYC20006282','HYYC20008933','HYYC20008935');

PATH-977 : Vendor Portal Actualization - Station Mapping Issue

Query :

For table :

select COUNT(DISTINCT SHPNO) SHIPCOUNT,SUM(FINALKGS) TOTWGT,ROUND(SUM(INVOICE_AMOUNT),0) SPEND,
COUNT(ONTIME) ONTIMECOUNT, ONTIME,BIZTYPE,QUATER, FINPERIOD
from CWL_OPS_QBR_REPORT_MV WHERE
PARTYID='AMER707CMH' AND JOBDATE >='01-01-20' AND  JOBDATE <='27-10-20'
GROUP BY BIZTYPE,ONTIME,QUATER,FINPERIOD  ORDER BY QUATER,BIZTYPE,ONTIME;

For Shipment Count and Tonnage by Quater - All modes

select COUNT(DISTINCT SHPNO) SHIPCOUNT,SUM(FINALKGS/1000) TOTWGT_TONE,FINPERIOD
from CWL_OPS_QBR_REPORT_MV WHERE JOBDATE >='01-01-20' AND  JOBDATE <='27-10-20'
GROUP BY FINPERIOD  ORDER BY FINPERIOD;

Total Spend by Quater All modules

select COUNT(DISTINCT SHPNO) SHIPCOUNT,ROUND(SUM(INVOICE_AMOUNT),0) SPEND_AMT_USD, FINPERIOD
from CWL_OPS_QBR_REPORT_MV WHERE JOBDATE >='01-01-20' AND  JOBDATE <='27-10-20'
GROUP BY FINPERIOD  ORDER BY FINPERIOD;

TOTAL INVOICING BY QUATER

select ROUND(SUM(INVOICE_AMOUNT),0) TOTALINVOICING, FINPERIOD,BIZTYPE
from CWL_OPS_QBR_REPORT_MV WHERE JOBDATE >='01-01-20' AND  JOBDATE <='27-10-20'
GROUP BY BIZTYPE,FINPERIOD  ORDER BY FINPERIOD,BIZTYPE;

Average days to Payments by Quater

select COUNT(DISTINCT SHPNO) SHIPCOUNT,
(SUM((PAID_DATE-INVOICE_DATE))/COUNT(DISTINCT SHPNO)) INVOICE, FINPERIOD
from CWL_OPS_QBR_REPORT_MV
WHERE  JOBDATE >='01-01-20' AND  JOBDATE <='27-10-20'
GROUP BY FINPERIOD ORDER BY FINPERIOD;

AVERAGE DAYS DELIVERY TO INVOICE CREATION BY QUARTER

select COUNT(DISTINCT SHPNO) SHIPCOUNT,
(SUM((ACT_DATE-INVOICE_DATE))/COUNT(DISTINCT SHPNO)) INVOICE, FINPERIOD
from CWL_OPS_QBR_REPORT_MV
WHERE JOBDATE >='01-01-20' AND  JOBDATE <='27-10-20'
GROUP BY FINPERIOD ORDER BY FINPERIOD;



Potential Exceptions Widget

This widget is designed and developed only for C-View and the data related to this widget is not from TMF or any other application data. 

We have a SQL SERVER database and store the data from the Portal admin for specific potential exceptions like natural disaster ot cyclone to a specific region

The relevant region approver will approve the potential exception to map the shipments related to the area covered on that region.

We have couple of tables to load all the information. First one is to add new potential exception by portal admin and waiting for approval. Second table will load all the realted shipments to that specific area.Both tables are loaded by approver.Third table is used to update the exception based on the shipments and Client ID associated.

POTENTIAL_EXCEPTIONS
POTENTIAL_EXCEPTIONS_SHIPMENTS
USERS

So far we have limited number of potential exceptions and single table to load the exception and its stright forwarded query.

We can add GSHPID and PARTYID ID index in the second table to improve the performence.

	IF(J33="TON",ROUNDUP(I33*1000,0),
	IF(J33="CBM",ROUNDUP(I33*333,0),
	IF(OR(J33="LBS",J33="LB"),ROUNDUP(I33*0.45359237,0),0))))),0,	IF(J33="KGS",ROUNDUP(I33,0),IF(J33="TON",ROUNDUP(I33*1000,0),
	IF(J33="CBM",ROUNDUP(I33*333,0),IF(OR(J33="LBS",J33="LB"),ROUNDUP(I33*0.45359237,0),0)))))

SELECT DISTINCT V.GSHPID,V.SHPNO,V.OWNERID,V.SHPTYPE,V.JOBNO,V.JOBDATE ,V.CONSOLNO, V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,
       Get_Delivered_Date (V.Gshpid) ACT_DELIVERED_DATE,  
        CASE WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('AE', 'AI','NJ') THEN V.POLCITY
              WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('SE', 'SI','IL') THEN V.PORCITY
			 END  AS POLCITY
         ,CASE WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('AE', 'AI','NJ') THEN V.POLNAME
          WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('SE', 'SI','IL') THEN V.PORNAME
         END  AS POLNAME
		 ,CASE WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('AE', 'AI','NJ') THEN V.POLCTRY
               WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('SE', 'SI','IL') THEN V.PORCTRY 
			 END  AS POLCTRY
        ,CASE WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('AE', 'AI','NJ') THEN V.PODCITY
              WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('SE', 'SI') THEN V.DESTCITY
              WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('IL') THEN V.DEVRYCITY
			 END  AS PODCITY
       ,CASE WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('AE', 'AI','NJ') THEN V.PODNAME
             WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('SE', 'SI') THEN V.DESTNAME
             WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('IL') THEN V.DEVRYNAME
			 END  AS PODNAME
        ,CASE WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('AE', 'AI','NJ') THEN V.PODCTRY
              WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('SE', 'SI') THEN V.DESTCTRY 
              WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('IL') THEN V.DEVRYCTRY 
			 END AS PODCTRY,V.SERVICELEVEL,V.SERVICEPLANTMPL,V.CUSTNAME,
		V.SHPRNAME,V.CSGNNAME,V.UNID, get_all_pod_remarks (V.gshpid) REMARK,V.PARTYID_CUST,V.PARTYID_SHPR,V.PARTYID_CSGN,
		V.CREATEBY	,V.CREATEDATE,	
        GET_MILESTONE_DATE(V.GSHPID,get_current_milestone_code_V2(V.GSHPID),'e') EST_DATE,
         GET_MILESTONE_TIME(V.GSHPID,get_current_milestone_code_V2(V.GSHPID),'e') EST_TIME,
          GET_MILESTONE_DATE(V.GSHPID,get_current_milestone_code_V2(V.GSHPID),'a') ACT_DATE,
           GET_MILESTONE_TIME(V.GSHPID,get_current_milestone_code_V2(V.GSHPID),'a') ACT_TIME,
            GET_MILESTONE_DATE(V.GSHPID,get_current_milestone_code_V2(V.GSHPID),'b') BROADCAST_DATE,
           GET_MILESTONE_TIME(V.GSHPID,get_current_milestone_code_V2(V.GSHPID),'b') BROADCAST_TIME,
		get_current_milestone_code_V2(V.GSHPID) MILESTONE,
        get_current_milestone_desc(V.GSHPID) MILESTONEDESC,        
        P.RELATED_PARTY_NAME,P.RELATED_PARTY_ID,V.SELLING_STATION,
        Get_Pod_Reason_Desc (V.Gshpid) REASONDESC ,
        NVL((SELECT OPUSERID FROM KEWILLFWD.JOBOTHER WHERE JOB_UNID = CWL_GET_UNID(V.GSHPID,'MAX')),'(N/A)') MAXOPUSERID ,
        V.OAGENT_NAME,V.BIZTYPE ,V.servicetype ,get_pod_reason_code(V.GSHPID) REASONCODE,
         CASE WHEN V.PROMISEDELVYDATE >=SYSDATE AND  (TO_CHAR(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DY') in ('SAT','SUN')) THEN  'DUE ON WEEKEND'
              WHEN  V.PROMISEDELVYDATE = SYSDATE THEN 'DUE TODAY'
              WHEN  V.PROMISEDELVYDATE = (SYSDATE+1) THEN 'DUE TOMORROW'
              WHEN (V.PROMISEDELVYDATE >=(SYSDATE-1) AND get_pod_reason_code(V.GSHPID) IS NULL ) THEN 'LNR'
              WHEN (V.PROMISEDELVYDATE >=(SYSDATE-1) AND get_pod_reason_code(V.GSHPID) IS NOT NULL ) THEN 'SERVICE FAILURES'
              ELSE 'FUTURE DELIVERIES'
        END STATUS,
      CASE WHEN (V.PROMISEDELVYDATE >= SYSDATE AND (TO_CHAR(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DY') in ('SAT','SUN'))) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END  "DUE ON WEEKEND"
      ,CASE WHEN V.PROMISEDELVYDATE = SYSDATE THEN 1 ELSE 0 END "DUE TODAY"
      ,CASE WHEN  V.PROMISEDELVYDATE = (SYSDATE+1) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END "DUE TOMORROW"
      ,CASE WHEN  (V.PROMISEDELVYDATE >=(SYSDATE-1) AND get_pod_reason_code(V.GSHPID) IS NULL )  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END "LNR"
      ,CASE WHEN (V.PROMISEDELVYDATE >=(SYSDATE-1) AND get_pod_reason_code(V.GSHPID) IS NOT NULL )  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END "SERVICE FAILURES"
      ,CASE WHEN  V.PROMISEDELVYDATE >=(SYSDATE+2) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END "FUTURE DELIVERIES"

	FROM CWL_SHIPMENT_STATUS_V  V, CWL_STATISTICAL_PARTY_V P 
WHERE
 V.JOB_UNID = cwl_get_unid(V.gshpid,'MIN')
AND V.PARTYID_CUST = P.RELATED_PARTY_ID (+)  
  AND V.PROMISEDELVYDATE <= (SYSDATE + 3)  
  AND (Get_Delivered_Date (V.Gshpid)  is null or( V.PROMISEDELVYDATE < Get_Delivered_Date (V.Gshpid)))
  And V.Promisedelvydate >= '01-jan-2015' 
  AND V.transhiptype is null
  and V.servicelevel != 'INVOICE' 
  and V.serviceplantmpl != 'INVONLY'  
  and V.jobno is not null
 -- AND get_pod_reason_code(V.GSHPID) IS NULL
 AND V.GSHPID='G0000000000003951197';
  and V.jobdate >= '01-Jan-2020';



  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "WEBPORTAL"."CWL_TC_SERVICE_FAILURE_V" ("GSHPID", "SHPNO", "OWNERID", "SHPTYPE", "JOBNO", "JOBDATE", "CONSOLNO", "PROMISEDELVYDATE", "ACT_DELIVERED_DATE", "POLCITY", "POLNAME", "POLCTRY", "PODCITY", "PODNAME", "PODCTRY", "SERVICELEVEL", "SERVICEPLANTMPL", "CUSTNAME", "SHPRNAME", "CSGNNAME", "UNID", "REMARK", "PARTYID_CUST", "PARTYID_SHPR", "PARTYID_CSGN", "CREATEBY", "CREATEDATE", "EST_DATE", "EST_TIME", "ACT_DATE", "ACT_TIME", "BROADCAST_DATE", "BROADCAST_TIME", "MILESTONE", "MILESTONEDESC", "RELATED_PARTY_NAME", "RELATED_PARTY_ID", "SELLING_STATION", "REASONDESC", "MAXOPUSERID", "OAGENT_NAME", "BIZTYPE", "SERVICETYPE", "REASONCODE", "STATUS", "DUE ON WEEKEND", "DUE TODAY", "DUE TOMORROW", "LNR", "SERVICE FAILURES", "FUTURE DELIVERIES") AS 
  SELECT DISTINCT V.GSHPID,V.SHPNO,V.OWNERID,V.SHPTYPE,V.JOBNO,V.JOBDATE ,V.CONSOLNO, V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,
       Get_Delivered_Date (V.Gshpid) ACT_DELIVERED_DATE,  
        CASE WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('AE', 'AI','NJ') THEN V.POLCITY
              WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('SE', 'SI','IL') THEN V.PORCITY
			 END  AS POLCITY
         ,CASE WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('AE', 'AI','NJ') THEN V.POLNAME
          WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('SE', 'SI','IL') THEN V.PORNAME
         END  AS POLNAME
		 ,CASE WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('AE', 'AI','NJ') THEN V.POLCTRY
               WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('SE', 'SI','IL') THEN V.PORCTRY 
			 END  AS POLCTRY
        ,CASE WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('AE', 'AI','NJ') THEN V.PODCITY
              WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('SE', 'SI') THEN V.DESTCITY
              WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('IL') THEN V.DEVRYCITY
			 END  AS PODCITY
       ,CASE WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('AE', 'AI','NJ') THEN V.PODNAME
             WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('SE', 'SI') THEN V.DESTNAME
             WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('IL') THEN V.DEVRYNAME
			 END  AS PODNAME
        ,CASE WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('AE', 'AI','NJ') THEN V.PODCTRY
              WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('SE', 'SI') THEN V.DESTCTRY 
              WHEN V.BIZTYPE IN ('IL') THEN V.DEVRYCTRY 
			 END AS PODCTRY,V.SERVICELEVEL,V.SERVICEPLANTMPL,V.CUSTNAME,
		V.SHPRNAME,V.CSGNNAME,V.UNID, get_all_pod_remarks (V.gshpid) REMARK,V.PARTYID_CUST,V.PARTYID_SHPR,V.PARTYID_CSGN,
		V.CREATEBY	,V.CREATEDATE,	
        GET_MILESTONE_DATE(V.GSHPID,get_current_milestone_code_V2(V.GSHPID),'e') EST_DATE,
         GET_MILESTONE_TIME(V.GSHPID,get_current_milestone_code_V2(V.GSHPID),'e') EST_TIME,
          GET_MILESTONE_DATE(V.GSHPID,get_current_milestone_code_V2(V.GSHPID),'a') ACT_DATE,
           GET_MILESTONE_TIME(V.GSHPID,get_current_milestone_code_V2(V.GSHPID),'a') ACT_TIME,
            GET_MILESTONE_DATE(V.GSHPID,get_current_milestone_code_V2(V.GSHPID),'b') BROADCAST_DATE,
           GET_MILESTONE_TIME(V.GSHPID,get_current_milestone_code_V2(V.GSHPID),'b') BROADCAST_TIME,
		get_current_milestone_code_V2(V.GSHPID) MILESTONE,
        get_current_milestone_desc(V.GSHPID) MILESTONEDESC,        
        P.RELATED_PARTY_NAME,P.RELATED_PARTY_ID,V.SELLING_STATION,
        Get_Pod_Reason_Desc (V.Gshpid) REASONDESC ,
        NVL((SELECT OPUSERID FROM KEWILLFWD.JOBOTHER WHERE JOB_UNID = CWL_GET_UNID(V.GSHPID,'MAX')),'(N/A)') MAXOPUSERID ,
        V.OAGENT_NAME,V.BIZTYPE ,V.servicetype ,get_pod_reason_code(V.GSHPID) REASONCODE,
          CASE WHEN (TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') >= TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy') AND  (TO_CHAR(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DY') in ('SAT','SUN'))) THEN  'DUE ON WEEKEND'
              WHEN TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') = TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy') THEN 'DUE TODAY'
              WHEN TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') = (TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy')+1) THEN 'DUE TOMORROW'
              WHEN (TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') < = (TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy')-1) AND get_pod_reason_code(V.GSHPID) IS NULL ) THEN 'LNR'
              WHEN  (TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') < = (TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy')-1) AND get_pod_reason_code(V.GSHPID) IS NOT NULL ) THEN 'SERVICE FAILURES'
              ELSE 'FUTURE DELIVERIES'
        END STATUS,
      CASE WHEN (TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') >= TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy') AND (TO_CHAR(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DY') in ('SAT','SUN'))) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END  "DUE ON WEEKEND"
      ,CASE WHEN TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') = TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END "DUE TODAY"
      ,CASE WHEN  TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') = TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy')+1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END "DUE TOMORROW"
      ,CASE WHEN (TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') < = (TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy')-1) AND get_pod_reason_code(V.GSHPID) IS NULL)  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END "LNR"
      ,CASE WHEN  (TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') < = (TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy')-1) AND get_pod_reason_code(V.GSHPID) IS NOT NULL )  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END "SERVICE FAILURES"
      ,CASE WHEN  TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'dd-MM-yyyy')>= TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY')+2  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END "FUTURE DELIVERIES"
	FROM CWL_SHIPMENT_STATUS_V  V, CWL_STATISTICAL_PARTY_V P 
WHERE
 V.JOB_UNID = cwl_get_unid(V.gshpid,'MIN')
AND V.PARTYID_CUST = P.RELATED_PARTY_ID (+)  
  AND V.PROMISEDELVYDATE <= (SYSDATE +3)  
  AND (Get_Delivered_Date (V.Gshpid)  is null or( V.PROMISEDELVYDATE < Get_Delivered_Date (V.Gshpid)))
  And V.Promisedelvydate >= '01-jan-2015' 
  AND V.transhiptype is null
  and V.servicelevel != 'INVOICE' 
  and V.serviceplantmpl != 'INVONLY'  
  and V.jobno is not null
  AND get_pod_reason_code(V.GSHPID) IS NULL
  and V.jobdate >= '01-Jan-2020';
  
  
  
    SELECT DISTINCT V.GSHPID,V.SHPNO,V.JOBDATE, V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,
       Get_Delivered_Date (V.Gshpid) ACT_DELIVERED_DATE,  
       get_pod_reason_code(V.GSHPID) REASONCODE,
          CASE WHEN (TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') >= TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy') AND  (TO_CHAR(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DY') in ('SAT','SUN'))) THEN  'DUE ON WEEKEND'
              WHEN TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') = TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy') THEN 'DUE TODAY'
              WHEN TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') = (TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy')+1) THEN 'DUE TOMORROW'
              WHEN (TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') < = (TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy')-1) AND get_pod_reason_code(V.GSHPID) IS NULL ) THEN 'LNR'
              WHEN  (TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') < = (TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy')-1) AND get_pod_reason_code(V.GSHPID) IS NOT NULL ) THEN 'SERVICE FAILURES'
              ELSE 'FUTURE DELIVERIES'
        END STATUS,
      CASE WHEN (TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') >= TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy') AND (TO_CHAR(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DY') in ('SAT','SUN'))) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END  "DUE ON WEEKEND"
      ,CASE WHEN TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') = TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END "DUE TODAY"
      ,CASE WHEN  TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') = TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy')+1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END "DUE TOMORROW"
      ,CASE WHEN (TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY') < = (TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'dd-mm-yyyy')-1) AND get_pod_reason_code(V.GSHPID) IS NULL)  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END "LNR"

      ,CASE WHEN  TO_DATE(V.PROMISEDELVYDATE,'dd-MM-yyyy')>= TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'DD-MM-YYYY')+2  THEN 1 ELSE 0 END "FUTURE DELIVERIES"
	FROM CWL_SHIPMENT_STATUS_V  V, CWL_STATISTICAL_PARTY_V P 
WHERE
 V.JOB_UNID = cwl_get_unid(V.gshpid,'MIN')
AND V.PARTYID_CUST = P.RELATED_PARTY_ID (+)     
  AND (Get_Delivered_Date (V.Gshpid)  is null or ( V.PROMISEDELVYDATE < Get_Delivered_Date (V.Gshpid))
  AND V.PROMISEDELVYDATE <   GET_MILESTONE_DATE(V.GSHPID,get_current_milestone_code_V2(V.GSHPID),'a')

SELECT *    
FROM  CWL_SAGE_AR_TRIAL_BALANCE_V
where AMTDUEHC != 0 AND INVOICE_NO='IVAE100501461';

select job_unid, VEHICLE,MODELDESC,CU,SERIAL,PLANKEY,PARTYID_CUST
from   ( select job_unid, refcode, ref_number,PARTYID_CUST,
                row_number() over (partition by refcode order by job_unid) as rn
         from   CWL_REFERENCE_NUMBER_V WHERE JOB_UNID='110000000006111629' and REFCODE in('PARTNO','CUSTLOC','CUST','SHPRLOC','SHPR') 
       )
pivot  ( min(ref_number) for  refcode in ('PARTNO' as VEHICLE,'CUSTLOC' as MODELDESC,'CUST' as CU,'SHPRLOC' as SERIAL,'SHPR' as PLANKEY)  );


select distinct job_unid,VE,CUL,CU,SHL,SH from (
SELECT distinct sno,refcode,no,job_unid
FROM CWL_REFERENCE_NUMBER_V WHERE JOB_UNID='110000000006111629'
and REFCODE in('PARTNO','CUSTLOC','CUST','SHPRLOC','SHPR') 
)pivot(
min(no) for refcode in ('PARTNO' as VE,'CUSTLOC' as CUL,'CUST' as CU,'SHPRLOC' as SHL,'SHPR' as SH) 
);

select * from
(
SELECT job_unid,REFCODE, ref_number,
--Decode(REFCODE,'PARTNO','VEC','CUSTLOC','LOC','CUST','CC','SHPRLOC','SL','SHPR','SL') REFTYPE,
partyid_cust 
FROM CWL_REFERENCE_NUMBER_V WHERE JOB_UNID='110000000006111629' and REFCODE in('PARTNO','CUSTLOC','CUST','SHPRLOC','SHPR')
)pivot(
 max(REFCODE) for REFCODE
 in (
    'PARTNO', 
    'CUSTLOC',
    'CUST',
    'SHPRLOC',
    'SHPR'
  )
  ); 

                I typically add _old to the invoice number so there is an audit trail (change 12345678 to 12345678_old).  This makes the invoice number/payee combination available to be used again.

                My suggestion here is to:

                1 – Make sure they invoice numbers are not in CWL_VP_COSTS.  If they are, they cannot use the same invoice number.
                2 – Update CWL_VP_STAGING and change the invoice numbers (for that vendor only) to ####_old (where #### is the original invoice number).
                3 – Have the vendor resubmit.

select a.ae_unid,j.gshpid, a.transaction,j.unid,a.job_unid,
  j.shpno,a.shpno 
         from kewillfwd.job j
          join kewillfwd.jobother o on j.unid = o.job_unid
          left outer join cwl_ae_actions a on j.unid = a.job_unid and a.action_type = 'Shipment with Loss'                   
        where j.unid = CWL_GET_UNID(j.gshpid,'MIN')
            and j.jobdate >= '01-Jan-2020'
            and j.shpno <> a.shpno;
			
			
 CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "WEBPORTAL"."CWL_MISSING_INVOICE_V" ("OWNERID", "SHPNO", "OAGENT_NAME", "GSHPID", "SHPTYPE", "JOBNO", "POLNAME", "POLCTRY", "PODCITY", "PODNAME", "PODCTRY", "PROMISEDELVYDATE", "JOBDATE", "SERVICELEVEL", "SERVICEPLANTMPL", "CUSTNAME", "SHPRNAME", "CSGNNAME", "UNID", "PARTYID_CUST", "PARTYID_SHPR", "PARTYID_CSGN", "CONSOLNO", "RELATED_PARTY_NAME", "RELATED_PARTY_ID", "SERVICETYPE", "BIZTYPE", "POLCITY", "SELLING_STATION", "FLTDATE", "INV_CUSTNAME", "INCOTERM", "KPI_ID", "PRODUCT_TYPE") AS 
  (
Select J.Ownerid, J.Shpno, (Select Fullname From Kewillfwd.Fmparty F Where J.Oagent = F.Partyid) Oagent_Name, 
        J.Gshpid, J.Shptype, J.Jobno, J.Polname, J.Polctry, J.Podcity, J.Podname,
        J.Podctry, O.Promisedelvydate, GET_MIN_JOBDATE(J.Gshpid) Jobdate, O.Servicelevel, O.Serviceplantmpl, J.Custname, J.Shprname, J.Csgnname,
        J.Unid, J.Partyid_Cust, J.Partyid_Shpr, J.Partyid_Csgn, J.Consolno, P.Statistical_Party_Name Related_Party_Name,
        P.Statistical_Party_Id Related_Party_Id, O.Servicetype, J.Biztype, J.Polcity, 
        Decode (O.Salesdept, Null, (Select Distinct  Selling_Station From Cwl_Selling_Station_V S 
                                    where s.ownerid in ('CWLPARENT', '*') and s.partyid = j.partyid_cust and s.rollup_station is not null),o.salesdept)  selling_station, 
        get_target_inv_date (j.jobno) fltdate, get_all_custname_iv (j.gshpid) inv_custname,
        o.incoterm,1,
        CASE WHEN (J.BIZTYPE IN ('AE', 'AI') AND (O.SERVICELEVEL !='WHS'  AND O.SERVICELEVEL !='CSTBKR')) THEN 'AIR'
WHEN (J.BIZTYPE IN ('SE', 'SI') AND (O.SERVICELEVEL !='WHS'  AND O.SERVICELEVEL !='CSTBKR')) THEN 'OCEAN'
WHEN (J.BIZTYPE IN ('IL')  AND (O.SERVICELEVEL !='WHS'  AND O.SERVICELEVEL !='CSTBKR'))  THEN 'GROUND'
WHEN O.SERVICELEVEL='WHS' THEN 'WAREHOUSE'
WHEN O.SERVICELEVEL='CSTBKR' THEN 'CUSTOMS BROKERAGE'
END PRODUCT_TYPE
From Kewillfwd.Job J Join Kewillfwd.Jobother O On J.Unid = O.Job_Unid And J.Voiddate Is Null And J.Shptype In ('H','D') -- And O.Serviceplantmpl != 'INVONLY'
                      Left Outer Join Cwl_Statistical_Party_V P On J.Partyid_Cust = P.Related_Party_Id 
                      Left Outer Join Cwl_Non_Kewill_Invoices Nk On J.Gshpid = Nk.Gshpid
Where J.Jobno Is Not Null
  And Nk.Gshpid Is Null
  and j.jobstagecode != 'C'
  And (P.Statistical_Party_Id  Is Null Or P.Statistical_Party_Id != 'INTERCO' )
--  And O.Serviceplantmpl != 'INVONLY'
 -- And J.Unid = (Select  Min(Unid) From Kewillfwd.Job  Where Gshpid = J.Gshpid  and voiddate is null and biztype != 'NJ'and jobno is not null  )  
  AND j.UNID = CWL_GET_UNID (j.Gshpid,'MIN')
  And (O.Frtterm Is Null Or O.Frtterm Not In ( 'FREIGHT COLLECT','Freight Payable at Destination', 'Freight Collect') )
  And j.jobdate >= '01-Jan-2019'
 --  And J.Gshpid = 'G0000000000000591390'
  And Get_Invoice_Count (J.Gshpid) = 0        
  and get_target_inv_date_v2 (j.jobno) < sysdate + 5
Union 
Select J.Ownerid, J.Shpno, (Select Fullname From Kewillfwd.Fmparty F Where J.Oagent = F.Partyid) Oagent_Name, 
        J.Gshpid, J.Shptype, J.Jobno, J.Polname, J.Polctry, J.Podcity, J.Podname,
        J.Podctry, O.Promisedelvydate, GET_MIN_JOBDATE(J.Gshpid) Jobdate, O.Servicelevel, O.Serviceplantmpl, J.Custname, J.Shprname, J.Csgnname,
        J.Unid, J.Partyid_Cust, J.Partyid_Shpr, J.Partyid_Csgn, J.Consolno, P.Statistical_Party_Name Related_Party_Name,
        P.Statistical_Party_Id Related_Party_Id, O.Servicetype, J.Biztype, J.Polcity, 
        Decode (O.Salesdept, Null, (Select Distinct  Selling_Station From Cwl_Selling_Station_V S 
                                    Where S.Ownerid In ('CWLPARENT', '*') And S.Partyid = J.Partyid_Cust And S.Rollup_Station Is Not Null),O.Salesdept)  Selling_Station, 
        get_target_inv_date (j.jobno) fltdate, get_all_custname_iv (j.gshpid) inv_custname,
        o.incoterm,1,
        CASE WHEN (J.BIZTYPE IN ('AE', 'AI') AND (O.SERVICELEVEL !='WHS'  AND O.SERVICELEVEL !='CSTBKR')) THEN 'AIR'
WHEN (J.BIZTYPE IN ('SE', 'SI') AND (O.SERVICELEVEL !='WHS'  AND O.SERVICELEVEL !='CSTBKR')) THEN 'OCEAN'
WHEN (J.BIZTYPE IN ('IL')  AND (O.SERVICELEVEL !='WHS'  AND O.SERVICELEVEL !='CSTBKR'))  THEN 'GROUND'
WHEN O.SERVICELEVEL='WHS' THEN 'WAREHOUSE'
WHEN O.SERVICELEVEL='CSTBKR' THEN 'CUSTOMS BROKERAGE'
END PRODUCT_TYPE
From Kewillfwd.Job J Join Kewillfwd.Jobother O On J.Unid = O.Job_Unid And J.Voiddate Is Null And J.Shptype In ('H','D') --And O.Serviceplantmpl != 'INVONLY'
                      Left Outer Join Cwl_Statistical_Party_V P On J.Partyid_Cust = P.Related_Party_Id        
                      Left Outer Join Cwl_Non_Kewill_Invoices Nk On J.Gshpid = Nk.Gshpid
Where J.Jobno Is Not Null
  And Nk.Gshpid Is Null
  and j.jobstagecode != 'C'
  And ( P.Statistical_Party_Id  Is Null Or P.Statistical_Party_Id != 'INTERCO' )
--  And O.Serviceplantmpl != 'INVONLY'
--  And J.Unid = (Select  max(Unid) From Kewillfwd.Job  Where Gshpid = J.Gshpid and voiddate is null and biztype != 'NJ' and jobno is not null )  
   AND j.UNID = CWL_GET_UNID (j.Gshpid,'MAX')
  And ( O.Frtterm In ( 'FREIGHT COLLECT','Freight Payable at Destination', 'Freight Collect') )
   And j.jobdate >= '01-Jan-2019'
--  And J.Gshpid = 'G0000000000000591390'
  And Get_Invoice_Count (J.Gshpid) = 0
  and get_target_inv_date_v2 (j.jobno) < sysdate + 5 
  );

myflixer.com
